fn test() {
    rand_seed(42);
    n = 20;
    v = rand_indices(n);
    assert(len(v) == n, "wrong size");
    // check every value 0..n appears exactly once
    for expected in 0..n {
        found = false;
        for x in v { if x == expected { found = true } }
        assert(found, "missing {expected}");
    }
}
